***обшить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обшить.html>обши́ть</a> (13529)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обшить.html>обши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obšítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обшива́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to edge, to border, to trim</li>
<li><i>(parcel, package etc)</i> to cover up</li>
<li>to plank, to revet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make clothes <i>(for)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:общак.html>обща́к</a> (29818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общак.html>обща́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obščák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общак.html>общака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общак.html>общаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общак.html>общако́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> common fund of a criminal group; mob money
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держатель.html>держа́тель</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:общак.html>общака́</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátelʹ <b>obščaká</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">gang's treasurer</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***общежитие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:общежитие.html>общежи́тие</a> (3334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbščij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to live</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общежитие.html>общежи́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obščežítije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общежитие.html>общежи́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общежитие.html>общежи́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общежитие.html>общежи́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dormitory</li>
<li>hostel</li>
<li>bunkhouse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> social life, common life, community
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Н. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a>. Березин, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:пешком.html>Пешко́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карельский.html>каре́льским</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водопад.html>водопа́дам</a></i> 1903:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>кругом</a> пустынника <a href = vnd.unilang:собираться.html>собира́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:братия.html>бра́тия</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вскоре.html>вско́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудовой.html>трудово́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:общежитие.html>общежи́тие</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расчищать.html>расчища́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса</a>, осуша́ли <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заводить.html>заводи́ли</a> хлебопашество <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслы</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krugom pustynnika sobirálasʹ brátija, i vskóre voznikálo trudovóje <b>obščežítije</b>, člény kotórovo óbščimi sílami rasčiščáli lesa, osušáli bolóta i zavodíli xlebopašestvo i prómysly</i></dd><dd>the brethren gathered in the wilderness and shortly a working <b>community</b> was formed whose members in joined tasks cleared forests, drained swamps and started tilths and fishing</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:общенародный.html>общенародный</a> (22449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naród</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общенародный.html>общенаро́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obščenaródnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nationwide, national <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">literally, "of all the people"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***общение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:общение.html>обще́ние</a> (3163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общение.html>обще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общение.html>обще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общение.html>обще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общение.html>обще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>communication, intercourse (concept of information exchange)</li></ol>

***общество.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщество</a> (450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">обьщьство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obĭštĭstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbščij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщество</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbštestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">општество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opštestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óbščestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бществ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>society
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщество</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:российский.html>росси́йских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желе́зных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́г</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Glávnoje <b>óbščestvo</b> rossíjskix želéznyx doróg</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The main society of the Russian railways</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>company</li>
<li>association</li>
<li>community</li></ol>

***общий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> (262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">обьщь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obĭštĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obьťь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о́бчий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óbščij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>обще́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>обще́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>common
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nas <b>óbščij</b> jazýk.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We share a <b>common</b> language.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nas <b>óbščij</b> interés.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We have a <b>common</b> interest.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>public</li>
<li>total, whole</li>
<li>general
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщих</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черта́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>óbščix</b> čertáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">roughly / in a general way</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v óbščem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all in all, by and large, generically, in general, on the whole</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> common
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">óbščij rod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">common gender, genus commune</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***община.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>община</a> (6341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (suffix-stressed) or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (stem-stressed).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obščína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>commune, collective society <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">primitive, often clan-based, society with collective ownership of the means of production</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> community of believers</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́на</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>о́бщина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obščína</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óbščina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́ны</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>о́бщины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́ны</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>о́бщины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>общи́н</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:община.html>о́бщин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>community</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объединение.html>объедине́ние</a> (5247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объединить.html>объедини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obʺjedinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объединение.html>объедине́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjedinénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объединение.html>объедине́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объединение.html>объедине́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объединение.html>объедине́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>association, union</li>
<li>unification</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> refers to a major combined field force such as a front or an army group (literally, unification, amalgamation, integration)</li></ol>

***объединяющийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объединяющийся.html>объединя́ющийся</a> (14729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объединяющийся.html>объединя́ющийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjedinjájuščijsja</span>)
</p>
